Oftentimes constituents have no idea what‚Äôs going on! And staffers have to explain why they‚Äôre suddenly on the phone with Congress.		Other times, the constituent goes rogue. Example: ‚ÄúSomebody called me and told me to tell you not to pass tax cuts, but I actually like tax cuts.‚Äù
These are called patch-through calls. They happen when an advocacy group dials a constituent and asks them about a particular policy issue, before patching them through to talk to a congressional office. Read @tonymecia and me on the tactic here: https://t.co/cuGz4nApzt
